BTW: the DONE state is your favorite state  :-)\r\n\r\nOn every Board there is another State: the OVERDUE state.  That's the worst state of all. If possible, it is recommended to avoiding the \"overdue\" state   ;)\r\n\r\nYou can NOT manually (via drag&drop) move a Task to the OVERDUE column. That will not work.
